Had a need to eliminate some Ants and Wasps in and around out house, so I went on Yelp to ask for quotes.  I asked Saturday, and received a couple of answers back slowly until Monday. I stated that Wednesday worked, and the technician (owner) scheduled something for 8-10am.  He was here promptly at 8am, and we walked the perimeter of the property (residential house) and talked about my pest control needs.  We identified problem areas, and the technician sprayed for ants, as well as a perimeter to prevent future infestations.  Offered to check inside, but I had no need at the time. <Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
This is a wonderful market specializing in Korean delicacies. I visited with the hopes that I would find everything to make a Korean BBQ style meal at home. I was not disappointed. In addition to a plethora of interesting imported items, I found thin sliced brisket, marinated spicy pork, and thin sliced pork belly. All of the meats look like great quality. They also carried several varieties of delicious kimchee and pickled radish. We even found our favorite Korean snack, banana puff chips. This is the best asian market that I've found in the Riverside area. I will definitely be back.</Review>

< user_name>

<gmap_id>0x80dcb0cee8d7b6eb:0x3f5337047626cf73<//gmap_id>< Review>
The prices are excellent, basically no different from the giant H-Marts in Orange County. The selection is well thought out. They know what all the best stuff is. I ask them for Korean food prep advice, and it works.

This is a lovely store run by a family who wants to bring accessible Korean groceries to the IE, a place they love and call home. They are living a good life and running an old-school family business. I like this place.

EDIT: This is the only meat I want to eat. Super clean and high quality cuts. Way cheaper than going to KBBQ. And you can drink at home, safe from the police.

EDIT: They make and sell their own kimchi recipe, and it's the best kimchi I have had in my life.</Review>

< Text>
I've been to Trout Creek Rec Center many times while renting summer houses in Tahoe Donner. It's a giant disappointment & really misses the potential it could have to be the only resort / rec center in the North Tahoe area. Here are the reasons why: the price is astronomical & sets the guest up to expect great things when paying the (reduced) rate of $15 per person (kids over age 6 have to pay the adult rate). Then, Trout Creek fails to meet even modest expectations. 1) staff ranges from unhelpful to rude. Need a towel? They're part of the price of admission, but they won't tell you that. They are kept behind the counter at the front desk. 2) As of 2019, the place is under massive construction & half of it is closed. They do not tell you this when taking your payment. What's worse? The construction is happening while the place is open. Buzz saws, hard hat areas, and literally a guy painting the ceiling as we walked under it! 3) The new sauna room smells like MRSA lying in wait 4) The pool itself is "kind of" clean in certain areas. In one large corner, pollen and dead bugs gather and it has always been this way. 5) Exercise classes are subpar; don't waste your money. I saw an instructor  doing leg lifts on all fours with a sway back. 6) The pool is cold all summer long.  One good thing about the facility is when Marco Polo Grill is open -- they offer poolside food service. It's fun and pretty tasty. However, they keep limited hours and don't open until late June.< /Text>

If you are going to breed them, please see a veterinarian prior to doing so and have regular checkups throughout their pregnancy, not only if/when things don't go as you had hoped. It is also very important to not self-treat or medicate your pet, pregnant or not, at home with medications that were intended for human consumption. <Review>Troy, Nathan, Jacob and the rest of the crew were outstanding and very hard-working! We had a clogged drain that ended up being a collapsed sewer pipe that needed replacing. The diagnostic person showed me the pipe using a camera and it was clear that the pipe needed replacement. I was offered three repair options and did not feel pressured to make a choice. There was no hard sell, which I appreciate.
Although my partner felt the repair price was high, I understand the difficulty of estimating a job like this since it is hard to predict what issues might come up underground - the job can go smoothly or be really challenging so it‚Äôs a bit of a gamble for both parties. Rooter Hero gives a fixed rate estimate for the job and does not add on extra fees as they go. This means the job price might be on the high end of the market, but it also avoids add in fees that can result in much high fees than estimated. Other companies give a base estimate and add on as they go. Considering that plumbing jobs can go south quickly, an open ended estimate can add up!
The job was done promptly and quickly. The crew was polite and careful of the plants and trees near the job and they always let us know what was up. The office was short staffed during the job so the paperwork follow up seemed slow but that is understandable. When my partner called the office and complained about the slow paperwork and that she thought the price was high, management quickly responded to make sure her complaints were satisfied. They explained the pricing strategy and sent photos and paperwork immediately. Troy came out personally to follow up. Responding quickly to customer issues is key, and this local Rooter Hero did a great job of following up! I would recommend them to anyone.</Review></record></dataset><record>

<Text>Words are not enough to describe how pleased I am with Rooter Hero Plumbing Sacramento, and the work they performed. Before contacting them, I had used another plumber who charged me about $700 to basically make a hole in a wall to access a pipe and then run a snake into it to temporary clear the pipes.  The problem returned a day later, but was worse.  After contacting several other plumbers to deal with the problem (some didn't return my call; some had phones that were disconnected; and others didn't have to proper equipment to handle the job), I finally got a hold of Rooter Hero and booked an appointment for the next day.  Much to my surprise, I received a phone call from the Operations Manager, Patrick, the following morning to assure me that he was sending over his best guy to troubleshoot the problem.  That guy turned out to be Greg, and Patrick was right about him.  After sending a camera into the pipes, we saw several failed sewer pipes leading from our house to the main sewer line.  No "snaking" was going to fix this problem. Greg immediately informed me as to what needed to be done and how. This it turns out was going to be a major project. After assuring me his company could handle this type of job, he wasted no time preparing and filing a work permit on his phone and scheduling a County Inspector to come out later that day.  Greg also sent out two guys, Antonio ("Tony") and Trever to dig the holes necessary to access the broken pipes.  These holes ended up going down about 15 feet.  Greg also determined a second hole could be dug outside my house to access the pipes connected to our downstairs bathroom toilet and shower instead of tearing up my bathroom and the adjacent laundry room and causing a major disruption to my family.  Throughout the entire project, which took a little less than two weeks, Greg, Tony and Trever worked diligently on completing the job with as little inconvenience to my family as possible.  They routinely worked long after dark, and on the weekends to finish the job as quickly as possible. They were all extremely courteous and professional and constantly kept me informed as to the status of the work. The work is now completed and we have complete use of our facilities again. The pipes are flowing like new!  I am absolutely convinced that had I not hired Rooter Hero or had Patrick, Greg, Tony and Trever not been involving throughout the repair, this situation would have been an absolute nightmare for me and my family.  I will be eternally grateful to all of them, and I will definitely use them again next I have any plumbing or other household problems!  Thank you! Thank you!
